110100000100100100000010000110100000000000000000000000010000000001010100000000000
Proof of non-3-colorability:
  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c1} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c1). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c1], r4c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c1]).
      → color(r1c2) = color(r4c1). Identify.
  3.  Diamond {r1c1, [r1c2=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1], r4c4} (spine [r1c2=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1]).
      → color(r1c1) = color(r4c4). Identify.
  4.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1], [r1c1=r4c4], [r1c2=r4c1], r4c2} (spine [r1c1=r4c4]—[r1c2=r4c1]).
      → color([r1c4=r2c1]) = color(r4c2). Identify.
  5.  Diamond {[r1c2=r4c1], [r1c1=r4c4], [r1c4=r2c1=r4c2], r2c4} (spine [r1c1=r4c4]—[r1c4=r2c1=r4c2]).
      → color([r1c2=r4c1]) = color(r2c4). Identify.
  6.  Diamond {[r1c1=r4c4], [r1c2=r2c4=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1=r4c2], r2c7} (spine [r1c2=r2c4=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1=r4c2]).
      → color([r1c1=r4c4]) = color(r2c7). Identify.
  7.  Diamond {[r1c1=r2c7=r4c4], [r1c2=r2c4=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1=r4c2], r3c5} (spine [r1c2=r2c4=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1=r4c2]).
      → color([r1c1=r2c7=r4c4]) = color(r3c5). Identify.
  8.  Diamond {[r1c1=r2c7=r3c5=r4c4], [r1c2=r2c4=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1=r4c2], r7c2} (spine [r1c2=r2c4=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1=r4c2]).
      → color([r1c1=r2c7=r3c5=r4c4]) = color(r7c2). Identify.
  9.  K₄ on {[r1c1=r2c7=r3c5=r4c4=r7c2], r8c3, r8c5, r8c7}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      → color(r1c1) = color(r5c4). Identify.

      → color([r1c4=r2c1]) = color([r4c5=r5c2]). Identify.
  9.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c1=r4c5=r5c2], [r4c7=r7c2=r8c5], r7c4, r7c5}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      → color(r1c2) = color(r4c1). Identify.
  3.  Branch on r6c3, r7c7:
      Case A: color(r6c3) = color(r7c7). Identify.
        4.  Diamond {r4c5, [r1c2=r4c1], r4c7, [r6c3=r7c7]} (spine [r1c2=r4c1]—r4c7).
            → color(r4c5) = color([r6c3=r7c7]). Identify.
        5.  Diamond {r4c7, [r1c2=r4c1], [r4c5=r6c3=r7c7], r7c2} (spine [r1c2=r4c1]—[r4c5=r6c3=r7c7]).
            → color(r4c7) = color(r7c2). Identify.
        6.  Diamond {[r1c2=r4c1], [r4c5=r6c3=r7c7], [r4c7=r7c2], r6c7} (spine [r4c5=r6c3=r7c7]—[r4c7=r7c2]).
            → color([r1c2=r4c1]) = color(r6c7). Identify.
        7.  Diamond {[r4c7=r7c2], [r1c2=r4c1=r6c7], [r4c5=r6c3=r7c7], r6c5} (spine [r1c2=r4c1=r6c7]—[r4c5=r6c3=r7c7]).
            → color([r4c7=r7c2]) = color(r6c5). Identify.
        8.  K₄ on {[r4c5=r6c3=r7c7], [r4c7=r6c5=r7c2], r5c4, r7c4}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color(r6c3) ≠ color(r7c7). Add edge.
        9.  Diamond {r6c5, r6c3, r6c7, r7c7} (spine r6c3—r6c7).
            → color(r6c5) = color(r7c7). Identify.
        10.  Diamond {[r1c2=r4c1], r4c5, r4c7, [r6c5=r7c7]} (spine r4c5—r4c7).
            → color([r1c2=r4c1]) = color([r6c5=r7c7]). Identify.
        11.  K₄ on {[r1c2=r4c1=r6c5=r7c7], [r1c4=r2c1], r5c4, r7c4}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  3.  Diamond {[r1c2=r4c1], r4c7, r4c8, r5c9} (spine r4c7—r4c8).
      → color([r1c2=r4c1]) = color(r5c9). Identify.

      → color(r1c1) = color(r5c4). Identify.
  5.  Diamond {[r1c2=r4c1=r5c9], [r1c1=r5c4], [r1c4=r2c1], r7c4} (spine [r1c1=r5c4]—[r1c4=r2c1]).

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

pattern 158/620: PROVED cells=14 depth=6 diamonds=8 branches=1 complete=true
110100000100000110000000000010100100000000010000000000010100010000000100000000000
Proof of non-3-colorability:
  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c1} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c1). Identify.
  2.  Branch on [r1c4=r2c1], r4c2:
      Case A: color([r1c4=r2c1]) = color(r4c2). Identify.
        3.  Diamond {r1c1, r1c2, [r1c4=r2c1=r4c2], r7c2} (spine r1c2—[r1c4=r2c1=r4c2]).
            → color(r1c1) = color(r7c2). Identify.
        4.  Diamond {r1c2, [r1c1=r7c2], [r1c4=r2c1=r4c2], r7c4} (spine [r1c1=r7c2]—[r1c4=r2c1=r4c2]).
            → color(r1c2) = color(r7c4). Identify.
        5.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1=r4c2], [r1c1=r7c2], [r1c2=r7c4], r7c8} (spine [r1c1=r7c2]—[r1c2=r7c4]).
            → color([r1c4=r2c1=r4c2]) = color(r7c8). Identify.
        6.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c1=r4c2=r7c8], r2c7, r4c7, r8c7}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color([r1c4=r2c1]) ≠ color(r4c2). Add edge.
        7.  Diamond {r1c1, r1c2, [r1c4=r2c1], r4c2} (spine r1c2—[r1c4=r2c1]).
            → color(r1c1) = color(r4c2). Identify.
        8.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1], [r1c1=r4c2], r1c2, r7c2} (spine [r1c1=r4c2]—r1c2).
            → color([r1c4=r2c1]) = color(r7c2). Identify.
        9.  Diamond {r1c2, [r1c1=r4c2], [r1c4=r2c1=r7c2], r4c4} (spine [r1c1=r4c2]—[r1c4=r2c1=r7c2]).
            → color(r1c2) = color(r4c4). Identify.
        10.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1=r7c2], [r1c1=r4c2], [r1c2=r4c4], r4c7} (spine [r1c1=r4c2]—[r1c2=r4c4]).
            → color([r1c4=r2c1=r7c2]) = color(r4c7). Identify.
        11.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c1=r4c7=r7c2], r2c8, r5c8, r7c8}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  4.  Diamond {r2c5, [r1c4=r2c3=r8c5], [r2c7=r3c5], r8c7} (spine [r1c4=r2c3=r8c5]—[r2c7=r3c5]).
      → color(r2c5) = color(r8c7). Identify.
  5.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c3=r8c5], [r2c5=r8c7], [r2c7=r3c5], r4c7} (spine [r2c5=r8c7]—[r2c7=r3c5]).
      → color([r1c4=r2c3=r8c5]) = color(r4c7). Identify.
  6.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c3=r4c7=r8c5], r4c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c3=r4c7=r8c5]).
      → color(r1c2) = color(r4c1). Identify.
  7.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c3=r4c7=r8c5], r1c1, [r1c2=r4c1], r7c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c2=r4c1]).
      → color([r1c4=r2c3=r4c7=r8c5]) = color(r7c1). Identify.
  8.  K₄ on {[r1c2=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c3=r4c7=r7c1=r8c5], r4c2, r7c2}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  2.  Branch on [r1c4=r2c3], r4c5:
      Case A: color([r1c4=r2c3]) = color(r4c5). Identify.
        3.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c3=r4c5], r4c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c3=r4c5]).

        5.  K₄ on {[r1c2=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c3=r4c5=r7c1], r4c2, r8c2}. Contradiction.

            → color([r1c4=r2c3=r5c2]) = color(r7c1). Identify.

            → color(r1c1) = color(r8c2). Identify.

            → color(r2c7) = color(r5c6). Identify.
        15.  K₄ on {[r2c7=r5c6], r4c5, r4c7, [r5c7=r6c4]}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c3). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {r2c7, [r1c4=r2c3], r2c5, r3c5} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—r2c5).

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

            → color([r1c4=r2c3=r7c5]) = color(r4c1). Identify.
        12.  K₄ on {[r1c2=r7c1=r8c6], [r1c4=r2c3=r4c1=r7c5], [r3c6=r5c5], r5c2}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      → color(r1c2) = color(r4c1). Identify.

      → color(r1c1) = color([r6c3=r7c4]). Identify.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      Case A: color(r5c5) = color([r7c1=r8c6]). Identify.
        4.  Diamond {[r5c5=r7c1=r8c6], r4c1, r5c2, r6c3} (spine r4c1—r5c2).
            → color([r5c5=r7c1=r8c6]) = color(r6c3). Identify.
        5.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c3], r4c4, [r5c5=r6c3=r7c1=r8c6], r7c4}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color(r5c5) ≠ color([r7c1=r8c6]). Add edge.
        6.  Diamond {r4c4, r5c5, r6c6, [r7c1=r8c6]} (spine r5c5—r6c6).
            → color(r4c4) = color([r7c1=r8c6]). Identify.
        7.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c3], [r4c4=r7c1=r8c6]} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c3]).
            → color(r1c2) = color([r4c4=r7c1=r8c6]). Identify.
        8.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c3], r1c1, [r1c2=r4c4=r7c1=r8c6], r4c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c2=r4c4=r7c1=r8c6]).
            → color([r1c4=r2c3]) = color(r4c1). Identify.
        9.  Diamond {r1c1, [r1c2=r4c4=r7c1=r8c6], [r1c4=r2c3=r4c1], r5c2} (spine [r1c2=r4c4=r7c1=r8c6]—[r1c4=r2c3=r4c1]).
            → color(r1c1) = color(r5c2). Identify.
        10.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c3=r4c1], [r1c1=r5c2], [r1c2=r4c4=r7c1=r8c6], r5c5} (spine [r1c1=r5c2]—[r1c2=r4c4=r7c1=r8c6]).

      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c3} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c3). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {r5c7, r6c8, r6c9, r6c3} (spine r6c8—r6c9).
      → color(r5c7) = color(r6c3). Identify.
  3.  Diamond {r5c4, [r1c4=r2c3], [r5c7=r6c3], r7c3} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—[r5c7=r6c3]).
      → color(r5c4) = color(r7c3). Identify.
  4.  Diamond {r4c1, r5c2, [r5c7=r6c3], [r5c4=r7c3]} (spine r5c2—[r5c7=r6c3]).
      → color(r4c1) = color([r5c4=r7c3]). Identify.
  5.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c3], [r4c1=r5c4=r7c3]} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c3]).
      → color(r1c2) = color([r4c1=r5c4=r7c3]). Identify.
  6.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c3], r1c1, [r1c2=r4c1=r5c4=r7c3], r7c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c2=r4c1=r5c4=r7c3]).
      → color([r1c4=r2c3]) = color(r7c1). Identify.
  7.  K₄ on {[r1c2=r4c1=r5c4=r7c3], [r1c4=r2c3=r7c1], [r5c7=r6c3], r7c7}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

Proof of non-3-colorability:
  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c3} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c3). Identify.
  2.  Branch on r5c2, r6c5:
      Case A: color(r5c2) = color(r6c5). Identify.
        3.  Diamond {r5c4, [r5c2=r6c5], r5c7, r6c7} (spine [r5c2=r6c5]—r5c7).
            → color(r5c4) = color(r6c7). Identify.
        4.  Diamond {r5c7, [r5c2=r6c5], [r5c4=r6c7], r6c3} (spine [r5c2=r6c5]—[r5c4=r6c7]).
            → color(r5c7) = color(r6c3). Identify.
        5.  Diamond {r4c1, [r5c2=r6c5], [r5c7=r6c3], [r5c4=r6c7]} (spine [r5c2=r6c5]—[r5c7=r6c3]).
            → color(r4c1) = color([r5c4=r6c7]). Identify.
        6.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c3], [r4c1=r5c4=r6c7]} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c3]).
            → color(r1c2) = color([r4c1=r5c4=r6c7]). Identify.
        7.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c3], r1c1, [r1c2=r4c1=r5c4=r6c7], r7c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c2=r4c1=r5c4=r6c7]).
            → color([r1c4=r2c3]) = color(r7c1). Identify.
        8.  K₄ on {[r1c2=r4c1=r5c4=r6c7], [r1c4=r2c3=r7c1], [r5c7=r6c3], r7c7}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color(r5c2) ≠ color(r6c5). Add edge.
        9.  Diamond {r5c7, r5c2, r5c4, r6c5} (spine r5c2—r5c4).
            → color(r5c7) = color(r6c5). Identify.
        10.  Diamond {r5c4, r5c2, [r5c7=r6c5], r6c3} (spine r5c2—[r5c7=r6c5]).
            → color(r5c4) = color(r6c3). Identify.
        11.  Diamond {r4c1, r5c2, [r5c4=r6c3], [r5c7=r6c5]} (spine r5c2—[r5c4=r6c3]).
            → color(r4c1) = color([r5c7=r6c5]). Identify.
        12.  K₄ on {[r4c1=r5c7=r6c5], r7c1, r7c5, r7c7}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

Proof of non-3-colorability:
  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c3} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c3). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c3], r5c3, r5c4, r5c7} (spine r5c3—r5c4).
      → color([r1c4=r2c3]) = color(r5c7). Identify.
  3.  Branch on r6c6, r7c1:
      Case A: color(r6c6) = color(r7c1). Identify.
        4.  Diamond {r4c7, r4c1, r4c5, [r6c6=r7c1]} (spine r4c1—r4c5).
            → color(r4c7) = color([r6c6=r7c1]). Identify.
        5.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c3=r5c7], [r4c7=r6c6=r7c1]} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c3=r5c7]).
            → color(r1c2) = color([r4c7=r6c6=r7c1]). Identify.
        6.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c3=r5c7], r1c1, [r1c2=r4c7=r6c6=r7c1], r4c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c2=r4c7=r6c6=r7c1]).
            → color([r1c4=r2c3=r5c7]) = color(r4c1). Identify.
        7.  K₄ on {[r1c2=r4c7=r6c6=r7c1], [r1c4=r2c3=r4c1=r5c7], r4c5, r5c4}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color(r6c6) ≠ color(r7c1). Add edge.
        8.  Diamond {r6c6, r7c1, r7c6, r7c7} (spine r7c1—r7c6).
            → color(r6c6) = color(r7c7). Identify.
        9.  Diamond {r5c3, [r1c4=r2c3=r5c7], r5c4, [r6c6=r7c7]} (spine [r1c4=r2c3=r5c7]—r5c4).
            → color(r5c3) = color([r6c6=r7c7]). Identify.
        10.  K₄ on {r4c1, r4c5, r4c7, [r5c3=r6c6=r7c7]}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c3} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c3). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {r4c5, r4c1, r4c2, r6c3} (spine r4c1—r4c2).
      → color(r4c5) = color(r6c3). Identify.
  3.  Diamond {r3c6, [r1c4=r2c3], r2c5, [r4c5=r6c3]} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—r2c5).
      → color(r3c6) = color([r4c5=r6c3]). Identify.
  4.  Diamond {r2c5, [r1c4=r2c3], [r3c6=r4c5=r6c3], r5c4} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—[r3c6=r4c5=r6c3]).
      → color(r2c5) = color(r5c4). Identify.
  5.  Diamond {[r2c5=r5c4], [r1c4=r2c3], [r3c6=r4c5=r6c3], r7c3} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—[r3c6=r4c5=r6c3]).
      → color([r2c5=r5c4]) = color(r7c3). Identify.
  6.  K₄ on {[r2c5=r5c4=r7c3], [r3c6=r4c5=r6c3], r5c6, r7c6}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  2.  Diamond {r2c7, [r1c4=r2c3], r2c5, r3c6} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—r2c5).
      → color(r2c7) = color(r3c6). Identify.
  3.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c3], r4c3, r4c4, r4c8} (spine r4c3—r4c4).
      → color([r1c4=r2c3]) = color(r4c8). Identify.
  4.  Diamond {r2c5, [r1c4=r2c3=r4c8], [r2c7=r3c6], r6c7} (spine [r1c4=r2c3=r4c8]—[r2c7=r3c6]).
      → color(r2c5) = color(r6c7). Identify.
  5.  Diamond {[r2c7=r3c6], [r1c4=r2c3=r4c8], [r2c5=r6c7], r5c8} (spine [r1c4=r2c3=r4c8]—[r2c5=r6c7]).
      → color([r2c7=r3c6]) = color(r5c8). Identify.
  6.  K₄ on {[r2c5=r6c7], [r2c7=r3c6=r5c8], r5c5, r6c6}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

Proof of non-3-colorability:
  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c3} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c3). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {r2c7, [r1c4=r2c3], r2c5, r3c6} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—r2c5).
      → color(r2c7) = color(r3c6). Identify.
  3.  Branch on [r1c4=r2c3], r5c7:
      Case A: color([r1c4=r2c3]) = color(r5c7). Identify.
        4.  Diamond {[r2c7=r3c6], [r1c4=r2c3=r5c7], r2c5, r5c5} (spine [r1c4=r2c3=r5c7]—r2c5).
            → color([r2c7=r3c6]) = color(r5c5). Identify.
        5.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c3=r5c7], [r2c7=r3c6=r5c5], r4c4, r4c7}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color([r1c4=r2c3]) ≠ color(r5c7). Add edge.
        6.  Diamond {r2c5, [r1c4=r2c3], [r2c7=r3c6], r5c7} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—[r2c7=r3c6]).
            → color(r2c5) = color(r5c7). Identify.
        7.  Diamond {[r2c7=r3c6], [r1c4=r2c3], [r2c5=r5c7], r5c3} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—[r2c5=r5c7]).
            → color([r2c7=r3c6]) = color(r5c3). Identify.
        8.  Diamond {[r2c5=r5c7], [r1c4=r2c3], [r2c7=r3c6=r5c3], r6c3} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—[r2c7=r3c6=r5c3]).
            → color([r2c5=r5c7]) = color(r6c3). Identify.
        9.  K₄ on {[r2c5=r5c7=r6c3], [r2c7=r3c6=r5c3], r5c5, r6c6}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

        6.  Diamond {[r4c4=r5c3], [r1c4=r2c3=r5c7], [r2c7=r5c6=r7c4], r7c7} (spine [r1c4=r2c3=r5c7]—[r2c7=r5c6=r7c4]).
            → color([r4c4=r5c3]) = color(r7c7). Identify.
        7.  K₄ on {[r2c7=r5c6=r7c4], [r4c4=r5c3=r7c7], r6c5, r7c5}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color(r2c7) ≠ color(r5c6). Add edge.
        8.  Diamond {r5c6, r2c7, r5c7, r7c7} (spine r2c7—r5c7).
            → color(r5c6) = color(r7c7). Identify.
        9.  Diamond {r6c5, r4c4, [r5c6=r7c7], r7c4} (spine r4c4—[r5c6=r7c7]).
            → color(r6c5) = color(r7c4). Identify.

            → color(r3c5) = color(r4c4). Identify.
        11.  K₄ on {[r3c5=r4c4], [r5c6=r7c7], [r6c5=r7c4], r7c5}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      → color([r1c4=r2c3]) = color(r4c7). Identify.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □
